All consumers MUST conform to this schema.\n     4→\n     5→| Field | Value |\n     6→|---|---|\n     7→| Schema Version | 1.0 |\n     8→| Source Decision | D-0003 (OQ-006) |\n     9→| Effective Release | v2.20 WorkflowEvolution |\n    10→\n    11→## YAML Frontmatter\n    12→\n    13→Every deviation report begins with YAML frontmatter:\n    14→\n    15→```yaml\n    16→---\n    17→source_pair: \"<upstream_file> → <downstream_file>\"\n    18→upstream_file: \"<path to upstream document>\"\n    19→downstream_file: \"<path to downstream document>\"\n    20→high_severity_count: <integer>\n    21→medium_severity_count: <integer>\n    22→low_severity_count: <integer>\n    23→total_deviations: <integer>\n    24→validation_complete: <boolean>\n    25→fidelity_check_attempted: <boolean>\n    26→tasklist_ready: <boolean>\n    27→---\n    28→```\n    29→\n    30→### Frontmatter Field Definitions\n    31→\n    32→| Field | Type | Required | Description |\n    33→|---|---|---|---|\n    34→| `source_pair` | String | Yes | Human-readable label: `\"<upstream> → <downstream>\"` |\n    35→| `upstream_file` | String | Yes | Relative path to the upstream (source/spec) document |\n    36→| `downstream_file` | String | Yes | Relative path to the downstream (generated) document |\n    37→| `high_severity_count` | Integer | Yes | Count of HIGH-severity deviations (≥0) |\n    38→| `medium_severity_count` | Integer | Yes | Count of MEDIUM-severity deviations (≥0) |\n    39→| `low_severity_count` | Integer | Yes | Count of LOW-severity deviations (≥0) |\n    40→| `total_deviations` | Integer | Yes | Total deviation count (must equal sum of severity counts) |\n    41→| `validation_complete` | Boolean | Yes | `true` if the fidelity check completed without errors |\n    42→| `fidelity_check_attempted` | Boolean | Yes | `true` if the fidelity check was invoked |\n    43→| `tasklist_ready` | Boolean | Yes | `true` only if `high_severity_count == 0` AND `validation_complete == true` |\n    44→\n    45→## Deviation Table Schema (7 Columns)\n    46→\n    47→The deviation table uses standard Markdown table format:\n    48→\n    49→| # | Column | Type | Constraints | Description |\n    50→|---|---|---|---|---|\n    51→| 1 | ID | String | Format: `DEV-NNN` | Unique deviation identifier, zero-padded 3-digit |\n    52→| 2 | Severity | Enum | `HIGH` \\| `MEDIUM` \\| `LOW` | Classification level |\n    53→| 3 | Deviation | String | Non-empty | Concise description of what differs |\n    54→| 4 | Upstream Quote | String | Non-empty | Verbatim quote from upstream document |\n    55→| 5 | Downstream Quote | String | Non-empty or `[MISSING]` | Verbatim quote from downstream document |\n    56→| 6 | Impact | String | Non-empty | Assessment of how deviation affects correctness |\n    57→| 7 | Recommended Correction | String | Non-empty | Specific action to resolve the deviation |\n    58→\n    59→## Column Name Rationale\n    60→\n    61→Generic names `Upstream Quote` / `Downstream Quote` are used instead of `Spec Quote` / `Roadmap Quote` because the fidelity check is reusable across document pairs (spec→roadmap, roadmap→tasklist). The frontmatter `source_pair` field provides specific document context.\n    62→\n    63→## Gate Interactions\n    64→\n    65→| Gate Check | Field Used | Logic | Blocking in v2.20 |\n    66→|---|---|---|---|\n    67→| `_high_severity_count_zero()` | `high_severity_count` | `True` if value is `0`; `False` if missing or >0 | Yes |\n    68→| `_tasklist_ready_consistent()` | `tasklist_ready`, `high_severity_count`, `validation_complete` | `True` if consistent | Yes |\n    69→| Count cross-validation | All severity counts vs table rows | Warning log on mismatch | No (warning only) |\n    70→\n    71→## Example\n    72→\n    73→```markdown\n    74→---\n    75→source_pair: \"spec.md → roadmap.md\"\n    76→upstream_file: \"spec.md\"\n    77→downstream_file: \"roadmap.md\"\n    78→high_severity_count: 1\n    79→medium_severity_count: 2\n    80→low_severity_count: 0\n    81→total_deviations: 3\n    82→validation_complete: true\n    83→fidelity_check_attempted: true\n    84→tasklist_ready: false\n    85→---\n    86→\n    87→# Deviation Report: spec.md → roadmap.md\n    88→\n    89→| ID | Severity | Deviation | Upstream Quote | Downstream Quote | Impact | Recommended Correction |\n    90→|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|\n    91→| DEV-001 | HIGH | Missing FR-019 | \"Cross-references must be validated\" | [MISSING] | No cross-ref integrity | Add FR-019 to Phase 2 |\n    92→| DEV-002 | MEDIUM | NFR timeout relaxed | \"120s hard limit\" | \"120s target, 600s timeout\" | Less strict measurement | Clarify per OQ-008 |\n    93→| DEV-003 | MEDIUM | Parameter renamed | \"spec_file\" | \"source_file\" | Import paths affected | Rename for consistency |\n    94→```\n    95→\n    96→## Versioning\n    97→\n    98→Schema version 1.0, effective for v2.20. Click CLI surface only.\n  - Parses CLI args and builds config objects.\n  - Delegates to executor functions.\n- `models.py`\n  - Small dataclasses for CLI config and agent selection.\n- `prompts.py`\n  - Pipeline orchestration.\n  - Builds ordered `Step` objects.\n  - Runs Claude subprocesses through shared pipeline infrastructure.\n  - Handles dry-run, resume, output sanitization, state persistence, validation auto-invoke.\n- `validate_*`\n  - Spec fidelity prompt builder pattern\n\n### Location\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/prompts.py`\n\n### Signature\n```python\ndef build_spec_fidelity_prompt(\n    spec_file: Path,\n    roadmap_path: Path,\n) -> str:\n```\n\n### What it does\nIt is a pure prompt builder. It does not read files itself and does not interpolate the file paths into the prompt body. The executor passes the actual files as step inputs.\n\n### How it works\nThe prompt:\n\n1. Frames the role:\n   - “You are a specification fidelity analyst.”\n\n2. Instructs comparison between:\n   - provided specification file\n   - generated roadmap\n\n3. Embeds explicit severity definitions:\n   - `HIGH`\n   - `MEDIUM`\n   - `LOW`\n\n4. Defines comparison dimensions:\n   - Signatures\n   - Data Models\n   - Gates\n   - CLI Options\n   - NFRs\n\n5. Requires YAML frontmatter with:\n   - `high_severity_count`\n   - `medium_severity_count`\n   - `low_severity_count`\n   - `total_deviations`\n   - `validation_complete`\n   - `tasklist_ready`\n\n6. Requires a deviation report body with fields:\n   - ID\n   - Severity\n   - Deviation\n   - Spec Quote\n   - Roadmap Quote\n   - Impact\n   - Recommended Correction\n\n7. Appends the shared `_OUTPUT_FORMAT_BLOCK` to force frontmatter-first output.\n\n### Key implementation detail\nEven though the function accepts `spec_file` and `roadmap_path`, the body does not use them directly. The actual file context comes from the step’s `inputs` in the executor:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/executor.py`\n\nThat’s the dominant prompt-builder pattern in this module: prompt functions are content-agnostic instructions; executor injects file context.\n\n## 3. `SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE` pattern\n\n### Location\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/gates.py`\n\n### Definition\n```python\nSPEC_FIDELITY_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[\n        \"high_severity_count\",\n        \"medium_severity_count\",\n        \"low_severity_count\",\n        \"total_deviations\",\n        \"validation_complete\",\n        \"tasklist_ready\",\n    ],\n    min_lines=20,\n    enforcement_tier=\"STRICT\",\n    semantic_checks=[\n        SemanticCheck(\n            name=\"high_severity_count_zero\",\n            check_fn=_high_severity_count_zero,\n            failure_message=\"high_severity_count must be 0 for spec-fidelity gate to pass\",\n        ),\n        SemanticCheck(\n            name=\"tasklist_ready_consistent\",\n            check_fn=_tasklist_ready_consistent,\n            failure_message=\"tasklist_ready is inconsistent with severity counts or validation_complete\",\n        ),\n    ],\n)\n```\n\n### Pattern used\nThis follows the general gate-definition style in the module:\n\n- module-level constant\n- pure data\n- declarative gate config\n- optional list of `SemanticCheck`\n- strict/standard tier encoded as string\n- frontmatter requirements + minimum line count + semantic validation\n\n### Semantic checks used\n`SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE` uses exactly two semantic checks:\n\n1. `high_severity_count_zero`\n2. `tasklist_ready_consistent`\n\n### Behavior\nThis gate blocks pipeline passage if:\n- any required field is missing\n- line count is too small\n- `high_severity_count != 0`\n- `tasklist_ready` is inconsistent with severity/validation status\n\n### Important nuance\nThe gate does permit degraded output when:\n- `high_severity_count: 0`\n- `validation_complete: false`\n- `tasklist_ready: false`\n\nThat passes because:\n- `_high_severity_count_zero()` returns `True`\n- `_tasklist_ready_consistent()` treats `tasklist_ready=false` as consistent\n\nThis degraded-mode behavior is explicitly exercised in tests.\n\n## 4. Semantic check functions\n\n### `_high_severity_count_zero()`\n\n#### Location\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/gates.py`\n\n#### Behavior\nIt:\n\n1. Parses YAML-ish frontmatter via `_parse_frontmatter(content)`\n2. Returns `False` if:\n   - frontmatter missing\n   - `high_severity_count` missing\n3. Parses `high_severity_count` as int\n4. Raises `TypeError` if value is non-integer\n5. Returns `True` only if count is exactly `0`\n\n#### Practical semantics\n- clean pass: `0`\n- degraded pass: also `0`\n- any actual HIGH deviation: gate fails\n\n---\n\n### `_tasklist_ready_consistent()`\n\n#### Location\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/gates.py`\n\n#### Behavior\nIt:\n\n1. Parses frontmatter\n2. Returns `False` if:\n   - no frontmatter\n   - missing `tasklist_ready`\n3. Interprets `tasklist_ready` case-insensitively as boolean text\n4. If `tasklist_ready` is `false`:\n   - returns `True` immediately\n   - meaning “not ready” is always internally consistent\n5. If `tasklist_ready` is `true`, then it requires:\n   - `high_severity_count` present and parseable\n   - `high_severity_count == 0`\n   - `validation_complete == true`\n\n#### Practical semantics\nConsistency rule is:\n\n```text\ntasklist_ready=true  =>  high_severity_count=0 AND validation_complete=true\n```\n\nAny violation returns `False`.\n\n### Supporting helper\nThese checks depend on:\n- `_parse_frontmatter(content: str) -> dict[str, str] | None`\n- same file:\n  - `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/gates.py`\n\n## 5. Deviation report format from Phase 2\n\n### Canonical format doc\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/docs/reference/deviation-report-format.md`\n\n### Key schema\nThe doc defines a canonical deviation report with:\n\n#### Frontmatter\n- `source_pair`\n- `upstream_file`\n- `downstream_file`\n- `high_severity_count`\n- `medium_severity_count`\n- `low_severity_count`\n- `total_deviations`\n- `validation_complete`\n- `fidelity_check_attempted`\n- `tasklist_ready`\n\n#### 7-column deviation table\n- `ID`\n- `Severity`\n- `Deviation`\n- `Upstream Quote`\n- `Downstream Quote`\n- `Impact`\n- `Recommended Correction`\n\n### Related Python data model\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/fidelity.py`\n\nThis defines:\n- `Severity` enum: `HIGH`, `MEDIUM`, `LOW`\n- `FidelityDeviation` dataclass with fields:\n  - `id`\n  - `severity`\n  - `deviation`\n  - `upstream_quote`\n  - `downstream_quote`\n  - `impact`\n  - `recommended_correction`\n\n### Important mismatch to note\nThe canonical doc is generic:\n- `Upstream Quote`\n- `Downstream Quote`\n\nBut the roadmap prompt currently asks for:\n- `Spec Quote`\n- `Roadmap Quote`\n\nAlso, the doc describes a markdown table, while `build_spec_fidelity_prompt()` asks for numbered entries with named fields rather than explicitly requiring a markdown table.\n\nFor Phase 4 reuse, that mismatch matters if you want roadmap→tasklist fidelity to align with the generic canonical schema.\n\n## 6.
